    <a id="36401" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="36403" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="36405" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#36405" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="36407" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36409" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36410" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#36410" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="36412" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="36414" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#34999" class="Function">dim-cube</a> <a id="36423" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#36356" class="Bound">X</a><a id="36424" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36426" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="36428" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36429" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#35648" class="Function">axis-cube</a> <a id="36439" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#36356" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="36441" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#36410" class="Bound">x</a><a id="36442" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="36444" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1607" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="36446" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36447" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#35648" class="Function">axis-cube</a> <a id="36457" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#36358" class="Bound">Y</a> <a id="36459" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="36460" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1807" class="Function">map-equiv</a> <a id="36470" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#36405" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="36472" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#36410" class="Bound">x</a><a id="36473" class="Symbol">)))</a>

  <a id="37472" href="foundation.structure-identity-principle.html#1341" class="Function">is-contr-total-Eq-structure</a>
    <a id="37504" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="37506" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="37508" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#37508" class="Bound">D</a> <a id="37510" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37511" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#37511" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="37513" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="37515" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4888" class="Function">type-UU-Fin</a> <a id="37527" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#37508" class="Bound">D</a> <a id="37529" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="37531" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#4826" class="Function">UU-Fin</a> <a id="37538" class="Number">2</a><a id="37539" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="37551" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37552" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#37552" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="37554" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="37556" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#14344" class="Function">equiv-UU-Fin</a> <a id="37569" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="37570" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#34922" class="Function">dim-cube-UU-Fin</a> <a id="37586" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#37466" class="Bound">X</a><a id="37587" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="37589" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#37508" class="Bound">D</a><a id="37590" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="37592" class="Symbol">→</a>

                  <a id="46175" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="46177" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#43997" class="Function">cube-cube-with-labelled-faces</a> <a id="46207" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#44737" class="Bound">Y</a><a id="46208" class="Symbol">)</a>
                  <a id="46228" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#44854" class="Bound">e</a> <a id="46230" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#44860" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="46232" href="finite-groups.quaternion-group.html#44922" class="Bound">a</a><a id="46233" class="Symbol">)))</a>
